msg:This hotel is simply the highlight of this trip. I think you can stay at the Lingang Artyzen Habitat Hotel when you go to Shanghai Haichang Oceanarium. I think I can give Artyzen Habitat Hotel a five-star rating for the following reasons: 1. The location is absolutely superior. It is only three or four hundred meters away from Exit 1 of Dishui Lake Station and three or four hundred meters away from the edge of Dishui Lake. There is an electric car rental station outside the door. It is six hundred meters away from the planetarium. It takes a few minutes to ride a bicycle to the door, so you can queue up at any time. There is a sponge park nearby with a children's playground, which is a great attraction. It is four kilometers away from Haichang Oceanarium and costs ten yuan to take a taxi. Believe me, don't live in the park. Five kilometers is a reliable distance. 2. The hotel has excellent management and the staff is warm and friendly. The hotel opened in 2022. It is very new, modern and smart. There is a microwave oven, four bottles of canned drinks are given for free, and there is a rich and delicious breakfast. There are luggage racks, makeup mirrors, makeup chairs, dining tables, coat racks, smart toilets, and sanitary ware is Kohler... It's so thoughtful! There are also floor-to-ceiling windows. The room is spacious and bright, and you can see the lake view at a glance. More importantly, the front desk sister Holly Luo helped me upgrade to a 61-square-meter one-bedroom and one-living room, which really surprised me! I was so happy that I had a sweet dream all night and was extremely happy. Holly Luo is a beautiful and kind person. She is beautiful and kind. Important things should be said three times. 3. Finally, I will give you some travel tips. Regarding the tickets for the planetarium, you must have confidence that you can queue up to buy tickets. If you queue up in the morning and fail to buy tickets, you can go again at 1 pm. There will always be tickets, and the security guard said that no matter whether you buy a refund on your mobile phone, the ticket office will always solve the problem of the people in the queue. Yachen Yueju is definitely convenient for you to walk or ride a bike to buy tickets, because it is really close. As long as you stay in this hotel, you can get tickets in minutes. Regarding renting a car to travel around the lake, I want to say that this attraction seems to be much more fun than the planetarium. This is really a great selling point. You can also have a picnic by the lake and set up a tent and a canopy. I didn't expect the lake to be so fun. I thought I would just stand by the lake and look around and pick up some stones, but I didn't pick up any. I rode around the lake. I was supposed to check out at 1 o'clock, but I asked the staff to move my luggage out at 2 o'clock. They were patient and I was really sorry to bother them all the time. In short, Artyzen Residences was worth 1500 yuan for 600-700 yuan. Come on, Artyzen Residences!
Facilities: First-class, new and smart
Hygiene: Clean
Environment: Beautiful
Service: All very enthusiastic, Holly Luo is the most beautiful one!
First round of mini bar: Yes, four bottles free

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Habitat Deluxe Twin
info:Stayed in August 2023

posted:Posted August 21, 2023
msg:At 9 a.m. on August 20, we dined at the Artyzen Habitat Hotel Lingang, Shanghai. The waiter arranged for us, two adults and three children, to dine in a non-dining area when it was full. There was a very unstable triangular desk lamp on the unfixed table at the scene (I didn't know whether it could be used normally or had other damage problems before the lamp broke). Our two young children were frightened on the spot. The hotel "Song Qi" who claimed to be the manager at the scene and "Du Ying" the security guard not only did not immediately come forward to care about the safety of the children, nor did they arrive at the scene immediately to deal with rearrangement of seats. Considering the safety risks of the children, we had no choice but to find a safe dining area and appease the children. They interfered with us repeatedly during our meal, but they were held responsible repeatedly and their words were intimidating and threatening, which seriously affected us. After we completed all the check-out procedures and during the understanding of the incident, we have been actively cooperating and left an important personal message, indicating that we will actively cooperate after settling the children. The aftermath of the incident. but"
"Mr. Song Qi" actually brought the security guard "Mr. Du Ying" with him and repeatedly used a threatening tone to prevent us from leaving the store. (The two young children were severely frightened.) The point is the so-called lobby manager "Song Qi" Without any justification, the husband asked us to compensate the lampshade for up to 1,200 yuan. This lamp is a three-no product and has no brand (the cost and depreciation cannot be traced). The hotel cannot determine whether the lamp was originally damaged. Secondly, the hotel is unwilling to provide a receipt for the desk lamp. Thirdly, the desk lamp on site has three legs that are not fixed. The table on which the desk lamp is placed is also not fixed. The desk lamp is placed at a height that any child can reach. The video provided by the hotel is only It can be said that I was on the edge when it fell.
After the incident, our two young children were extremely emotionally unstable, so we had no choice but to cancel all subsequent itineraries booked by our companions (a total of 12 people).
We express doubts about the safety of the hotel's dining area, as well as our dissatisfaction with the service attitude of the hotel staff and their behavior of blackmailing guests.
When we left, the hotel did not give an explanation about the safety issues in their dining area, and insisted that they would pursue legal action to sue us. We were very angry. Let me ask, is such a service attitude worthy of such a hotel price? ?
